## Instruction

Based on the provided file `Market_Data.xlsx`, calculate the year-over-year growth rate percentage for each segment from 2015 to 2024 according to the segment/source mapping provided in the `Methodology` sheet (rounded to one decimal place), and save the results to a new Excel file named `segment_growth_rates.xlsx` where the first column is `Year` and the subsequent columns are the exact names (excluding `Total`) of segments arranged in the same order as they appear in rows in the `Methodology` sheet.

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
from openpyxl import load_workbook, Workbook
from pathlib import Path

src_path = Path('/workspace/dumps/workspace/Market_Data.xlsx')
wb = load_workbook(src_path, data_only=True)

# Read Methodology mapping
mws = wb['Methodology']
# Header categories in C2:Q2
categories = []
for col in range(3, 18):
    categories.append(mws.cell(row=2, column=col).value)

# Segment rows: from row 4 to row 13 (exclude row 14 Total)
segments = []
segment_weights = {}
for r in range(4, 14):
    seg_name = mws.cell(row=r, column=2).value
    if seg_name is None:
        continue
    if seg_name == 'Total':
        continue
    segments.append(seg_name)
    weights = {}
    for idx, col in enumerate(range(3, 18)):
        w = mws.cell(row=r, column=col).value
        if isinstance(w, (int, float)):
            if w != 0:
                cat = categories[idx]
                weights[cat] = w
    segment_weights[seg_name] = weights

# Read RawData
rws = wb['RawData']
# RawData headers in row 4: B4..Q4 correspond to categories list
raw_headers = {}
for idx, col in enumerate(range(2, 18)):
    name = rws.cell(row=4, column=col).value
    raw_headers[name] = col

# Build category time series mapping: cat_name -> {year: value}
cat_series = {}
# Determine available years in column A starting from row 5 until empty
row = 5
years = []
while True:
    y = rws.cell(row=row, column=1).value
    if y is None:
        break
    if not isinstance(y, (int, float)):
        break
    years.append(int(y))
    row += 1

for cat in categories:
    col = raw_headers.get(cat)
    if col is None:
        continue
    ser = {}
    for i, y in enumerate(years, start=5):
        val = rws.cell(row=i, column=col).value
        # Ensure numeric values only
        if isinstance(val, (int, float)):
            ser[int(rws.cell(row=i, column=1).value)] = float(val)
        else:
            ser[int(rws.cell(row=i, column=1).value)] = None
    cat_series[cat] = ser

# Compute segment values per year
segment_values = {seg: {} for seg in segments}
for seg in segments:
    weights = segment_weights[seg]
    for y in years:
        total = 0.0
        has_any = False
        for cat, w in weights.items():
            v = cat_series.get(cat, {}).get(y)
            if v is None:
                total = None
                has_any = False
                break
            total += w * v
            has_any = True
        segment_values[seg][y] = total if has_any else None

# Compute YOY growth % for 2015..2024
start_year, end_year = 2015, 2024
output_years = list(range(start_year, end_year+1))
results = []
header = ['Year'] + segments
results.append(header)
for y in output_years:
    row_vals = [y]
    for seg in segments:
        curr = segment_values[seg].get(y)
        prev = segment_values[seg].get(y-1)
        if curr is None or prev is None or prev == 0:
            row_vals.append(None)
        else:
            yoy = (curr - prev) / prev * 100.0
            row_vals.append(round(yoy, 1))
    results.append(row_vals)

# Write to new workbook
out_wb = Workbook()
ws = out_wb.active
ws.title = 'Segment YoY Growth'
for r_idx, row in enumerate(results, start=1):
    for c_idx, val in enumerate(row, start=1):
        ws.cell(row=r_idx, column=c_idx, value=val)

out_path = Path('/workspace/dumps/workspace/segment_growth_rates.xlsx')
out_wb.save(out_path)
print('Saved to', out_path)
print('Headers:', header)
print('Years:', output_years[:3], '...', output_years[-3:]) code
```

Years: [2015, 2016, 2017] ... [2022, 2023, 2024]
=== EXECUTION INFO ===

Execution time: 0.249 seconds
Timeout limit: 120 seconds

<div className="thinking-box">
🧐`Agent`

I have created the file segment_growth_rates.xlsx in the workspace with the requested year-over-year growth rates.

What I did:
- Parsed the Methodology sheet to build the segment-to-source mapping and weights (excluding the “Total” row).
- Used the RawData sheet to get annual values per source.
- Computed each segment’s annual value as the weighted sum of its mapped sources.
- Calculated YoY growth rates for 2015–2024 and rounded to one decimal place.
- Saved results with the first column as Year and subsequent columns as the exact segment names in the same row order from the Methodology sheet.

Output file:
- Path: /workspace/dumps/workspace/segment_growth_rates.xlsx
- Sheet: Segment YoY Growth
- Columns: Year, Auto OEM, Auto Components, Coil, Industry, ACE, Appliance, AlFi, CF, Food, Aero

Note:
- Cells are left blank where growth cannot be computed (e.g., missing underlying data or missing prior-year value).
